Environment: The small environment is okay, but the external environment, don‚Äôt expect the management ability of Red Star Macalline. The Vientiane City diagonally opposite is better.
Service: The guy at the front desk has a very clear mind and answers irrelevant questions. He is a good person. The cleaning aunts are very good.

*Sound insulation: bad review! The sound insulation of the glass of the large floor-to-ceiling windows is qualified, and there is almost no noise from the road. There is a lot of noise from inside the hotel, babies crying in the middle of the night, guests chatting in the middle of the night, children playing in the early morning, and cleaning aunts talking in the morning.
*Parking: Difficult! And there is an additional charge (not expensive, capped at 56 yuan/day).

Comprehensive evaluation: This hotel is really not worthy of "S". As a hotel with a price of more than 1200/room/night, the management details can be said to be "unqualified".

Like it: The laundry detergent in the small package is good. It can be seen that it is suitable for business travel, it is really a hotel, come back late and leave early.
